She had to run many floors by herself and was too busy. Please let me understand. How can I understand? Finally, the quilt was delivered after eleven o'clock! On the second night, I asked for two bottles of water, but they were not delivered until I went to bed. I called again the next morning and it was delivered! In addition, we stayed for two nights in total. The first night was booked on Ctrip.com and the other night was booked by a travel agency. We decided to check in on the first night. We had already said at the front desk that we would stay for two consecutive nights. We asked to help check whether there was an order for the other night and whether we needed to move. The answer was that there was an order and we could stay consecutively without moving. When we returned to the hotel at the end of the trip the next day, we went up to the room, but the card could not be swiped into the room. We had to go downstairs to find the front desk again. Isn't it a consecutive stay? Why did the room card swipe for me for one night? Speechless! I stayed in Northeast China for eight nights. For the other six nights, other hotels would not take more than ten minutes to get my things! Actually, the hotel's hardware facilities are really good, but I think the service should be improved. msg:How did this five-star hotel get the rating? It looks like a five-star hotel from the outside, but there is no reception at the gate, no service reception, and you have to go to the front desk to check in. The room facilities are old, and there is dust on the sofa. It feels like no one has stayed there for a long time. The TV in the room is actually a small-sized LCD TV. It is not even as big as the TV in the homestay.
I checked in during the May Day holiday. There were many wedding banquets in the hotel. The elevators for the guest rooms and the wedding hall were not separated. It was quite difficult to enter and exit the hotel.
Let's talk about the room cleaning service. Normally, check out is at noon. I went out in the morning and came back at about 10 o'clock. I found that the door of the guest room was open and there was no one inside. Fortunately, I took my things away when I left in the morning. I shouted a few times before I saw the waiter coming out of another room. I explained that it was the room cleaning, and I opened the door to get the tools. People who have stayed in a hotel know that the room cleaning is to push a tool cart and park it at the door of the room to be cleaned. The most important thing is that I stayed for one day, and I had not checked out at that time. The waiter must not be unaware. Fortunately, I booked a day in this hotel.
